\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/commit/758d28c8a2d5c9567158e339326b765f72da983e}{\texttt{{\ttfamily 758d28c8a}}} (\href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/pull/10390}{\texttt{\#10390}}) Core plugin permissions are now prefixed with {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecore}{core}:\+}, the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecore}{core}:\+default} permission set can now be used and the {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecore}{core}} plugin name is reserved. The {\ttfamily tauri migrate} tool will automate the migration process, which involves prefixing all {\ttfamily app}, {\ttfamily event}, {\ttfamily image}, {\ttfamily menu}, {\ttfamily path}, {\ttfamily resources}, {\ttfamily tray}, {\ttfamily webview} and {\ttfamily window} permissions with {\ttfamily \doxylink{namespacecore}{core}:\+}.
\item \href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/commit/7ba67b4aca8d3f3b1aa5ad08819605029d36e6b4}{\texttt{{\ttfamily 7ba67b4ac}}}(\href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/pull/10437}{\texttt{\#10437}}) {\ttfamily ios dev} and {\ttfamily android dev} now uses localhost for the development server unless running on an i\+OS device, which still requires connecting to the public network address. To conditionally check this on your frontend framework\textquotesingle{}s configuration you can check for the existence of the {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+HOST} environment variable instead of checking if the target is i\+OS or Android (previous recommendation).
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10266}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\+[2.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+23]\+}{\+[2.\+0.\+0-\/beta.\+23]\+}}\label{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10266}

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10353}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10353}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/commit/8de308d1bf6a855d7a26af58bd0e744938ba47d8}{\texttt{{\ttfamily 8de308d1}}}(\href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/pull/8723}{\texttt{\#8723}}) Restructured Tauri config per \href{https://github.com/tauri-apps/rfcs/blob/f3e82a6b0c5390401e855850d47dc7b7d9afd684/texts/0005-tauri-config-restructure.md}{\texttt{RFC\#5}}:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Moved {\ttfamily package.\+product\+Name}, {\ttfamily package.\+version} and {\ttfamily tauri.\+bundle.\+identifier} fields to the top-\/level.
\item Removed {\ttfamily package} object.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily tauri} object to {\ttfamily app}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily tauri.\+bundle} object to the top-\/level.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily build.\+dist\+Dir} field to {\ttfamily frontend\+Dist}.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily build.\+dev\+Path} field to {\ttfamily dev\+Url} and will no longer accepts paths, it will only accept URLs.
\item Moved {\ttfamily tauri.\+pattern} to {\ttfamily app.\+security.\+pattern}.
\item Removed {\ttfamily tauri.\+bundle.\+updater} object, and its fields have been moved to the updater plugin under {\ttfamily plugins.\+updater} object.
\item Moved {\ttfamily build.\+with\+Global\+Tauri} to {\ttfamily app.\+with\+Global\+Tauri}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily tauri.\+bundle.\+dmg} object to {\ttfamily bundle.\+mac\+OS.\+dmg}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily tauri.\+bundle.\+deb} object to {\ttfamily bundle.\+linux.\+deb}.
\item Moved {\ttfamily tauri.\+bundle.\+appimage} object to {\ttfamily bundle.\+linux.\+appimage}.
\item Removed all license fields from each bundle configuration object and instead added {\ttfamily bundle.\+license} and {\ttfamily bundle.\+license\+File}.
\item Renamed {\ttfamily App\+Url} to {\ttfamily Frontend\+Dist} and refactored its variants to be more explicit.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10354}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\+[2.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+21]\+}{\+[2.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+21]\+}}\label{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10354}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/commit/4f73057e6fd4c137bc112367fb91f5fc0c8a39f6}{\texttt{{\ttfamily 4f73057e}}}(\href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/pull/8486}{\texttt{\#8486}}) Removed {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+ENV\+\_\+\+PLATFORM\+\_\+\+TYPE} which will not be set for CLI hook commands anymore, use {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+ENV\+\_\+\+PLATFORM} instead. Also Changed value of {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+ENV\+\_\+\+PLATFORM} and {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+ENV\+\_\+\+ARCH} values to match the target triple more accurately:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily darwin} and {\ttfamily androideabi} are no longer replaced with {\ttfamily macos} and {\ttfamily android} in {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+ENV\+\_\+\+PLATFORM}.
\item {\ttfamily i686} and {\ttfamily i586} are no longer replaced with {\ttfamily x86} in {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+ENV\+\_\+\+ARCH}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10360}{}\doxysection{\texorpdfstring{\+[2.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+20]\+}{\+[2.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+20]\+}}\label{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10360}

\item Upgraded to {\ttfamily tauri-\/cli@2.\+0.\+0-\/alpha.\+16}
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10376}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md_tools_2_m_y_t_h_o_s_2app_2node__modules_2_0dtauri-apps_2cli_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md10376}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/commit/8b166e9bf82e69ddb3200a3a825614980bd8d433}{\texttt{{\ttfamily 8b166e9b}}}(\href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/pull/7949}{\texttt{\#7949}}) Changed a number of environment variables used by tauri CLI for consistency and clarity:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+PRIVATE\+\_\+\+KEY} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+SIGNING\+\_\+\+PRIVATE\+\_\+\+KEY}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+KEY\+\_\+\+PASSWORD} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+SIGNING\+\_\+\+PRIVATE\+\_\+\+KEY\+\_\+\+PASSWORD}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+SKIP\+\_\+\+DEVSERVER\+\_\+\+CHECK} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+CLI\+\_\+\+NO\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+SERVER\+\_\+\+WAIT}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+SERVER\+\_\+\+PORT} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+CLI\+\_\+\+PORT}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+PATH\+\_\+\+DEPTH} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+CLI\+\_\+\+CONFIG\+\_\+\+DEPTH}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+FIPS\+\_\+\+COMPLIANT} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+BUNDLER\+\_\+\+WIX\+\_\+\+FIPS\+\_\+\+COMPLIANT}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+DEV\+\_\+\+WATCHER\+\_\+\+IGNORE\+\_\+\+FILE} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+CLI\+\_\+\+WATCHER\+\_\+\+IGNORE\+\_\+\+FILENAME}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+TRAY} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+LINUX\+\_\+\+AYATANA\+\_\+\+APPINDICATOR}
\item {\ttfamily TAURI\+\_\+\+APPLE\+\_\+\+DEVELOPMENT\+\_\+\+TEAM} -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} {\ttfamily APPLE\+\_\+\+DEVELOPMENT\+\_\+\+TEAM}
\end{DoxyItemize}
\item \href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/commit/4caa1cca990806f2c2ef32d5dabaf56e82f349e6}{\texttt{{\ttfamily 4caa1cca}}}(\href{https://www.github.com/tauri-apps/tauri/pull/7990}{\texttt{\#7990}}) The {\ttfamily tauri plugin} subcommand is receving a couple of consitency and quality of life improvements:\+
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Renamed {\ttfamily tauri plugin android/\+ios add} command to {\ttfamily tauri plugin android/\+ios init} to match the {\ttfamily tauri plugin init} command.
\item Removed the {\ttfamily -\/n/\+-\/-\/name} argument from the {\ttfamily tauri plugin init}, {\ttfamily tauri plugin android/\+ios init}, and is now parsed from the first positional argument.
\item Added {\ttfamily tauri plugin new} to create a plugin in a new directory.
\item Changed {\ttfamily tauri plugin init} to initalize a plugin in an existing directory (defaults to current directory) instead of creating a new one.
\item Changed {\ttfamily tauri plugin init} to NOT generate mobile projects by default, you can opt-\/in to generate them using {\ttfamily -\/-\/android} and {\ttfamily -\/-\/ios} flags or {\ttfamily -\/-\/mobile} flag or initalize them later using {\ttfamily tauri plugin android/\+ios init}.
\end{DoxyItemize}
